Task instruction sent to agent 
# [VS Code] Fix Stale TypeScript Diagnostics After Git Branch Switch

**Repository:** microsoft/vscode  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** big_code_feature
**Task Type:** Feature Implementation - Large Codebase

**Reference:** [Trevor's Big Code Research](../../../docs/TREVOR_RESEARCH_DEC2025.md#1-vs-code-stale-diagnostics-after-git-branch-switch)

## Description

Users are seeing stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer have errors still show the old errors until the user manually opens each file and makes an edit. It seems like the diagnostics pipeline only refreshes on in-editor changes and misses file-on-disk changes from Git operations.

## Task

This task requires implementing code changes to fix stale diagnostics.

### Required Implementation

Check the full diagnostics flow from a text change through the extension host to the Problems view, identify where file system changes should trigger diagnostic updates, and propose where we'd need to add listeners to fix this.

### Implementation Steps

1. **Understand the diagnostics pipeline**:
   - Find the main diagnostics collection and how it stores errors per file
   - Locate the extension host communication for sending diagnostics to the client
   - Find the Problems view panel and how it subscribes to diagnostics
   - Look for existing file change listeners (e.g., `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile`, `onWillChange`)

2. **Identify where diagnostics are currently refreshed**:
   - Find the text change event handlers that trigger re-diagnostics
   - Understand how the diagnostics pipeline reacts to document changes
   - Look for any existing file system watchers or listeners

3. **Add file system change triggers**:
   - Add listener for file changes on disk (e.g., from `git checkout`)
   - Trigger diagnostics refresh for changed files
   - Clear stale diagnostics for files that no longer exist
   - Re-run TypeScript/language server analysis for affected files

4. **Test the fix**:
   - Switch branches that change TypeScript errors
   - Verify stale diagnostics are cleared
   - Verify new errors are shown after branch switch
   - No duplicate diagnostics appear

5. **Verify no regressions**:
   - All tests pass: `npm test`
   - No performance regression from additional file watchers
   - Diagnostics still work for in-editor changes

## Success Criteria

[x] Stale diagnostics are cleared when files change on disk  
[x] New diagnostics appear after Git branch switch  
[x] Diagnostics refresh without requiring manual file edits  
[x] Problems panel reflects current state of files  
[x] All tests pass: `npm test`  
[x] No performance regression  
[x] Code follows VS Code conventions and patterns

   222→	private static _compareIndexedTuplesByUri(a: [vscode.Uri, readonly vscode.Diagnostic[]], b: [vscode.Uri, readonly vscode.Diagnostic[]]): number {
   223→		if (a[0].toString() < b[0].toString()) {
   224→			return -1;
   225→		} else if (a[0].toString() > b[0].toString()) {
   226→			return 1;
   227→		} else {
   228→			return 0;
   229→		}
   230→	}

    16→function diagnosticsEquals(a: vscode.Diagnostic, b: vscode.Diagnostic): boolean {
    17→	if (a === b) {
    18→		return true;
    19→	}
    20→
    21→	return a.code === b.code
    22→		&& a.message === b.message
    23→		&& a.severity === b.severity
    24→		&& a.source === b.source
    25→		&& a.range.isEqual(b.range)
    26→		&& arrays.equals(a.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, b.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, (a, b) => {
    27→			return a.message === b.message
    28→				&& a.location.range.isEqual(b.location.range)
    29→				&& a.location.uri.fsPath === b.location.uri.fsPath;
    30→		})
    31→		&& arrays.equals(a.tags || arrays.empty, b.tags || arrays.empty);
    32→}

   109→	private getSuggestionDiagnostics(settings: DiagnosticSettings) {
   110→		const enableSuggestions = settings.getEnableSuggestions(this.language);
   111→		return this.get(DiagnosticKind.Suggestion).filter(x => {
   112→			if (!enableSuggestions) {
   113→				// Still show unused
   114→				return x.tags && (x.tags.includes(vscode.DiagnosticTag.Unnecessary) || x.tags.includes(vscode.DiagnosticTag.Deprecated));
   115→			}
   116→			return true;
   117→		});
   118→	}

   252→	private configFileDiagnosticsReceived(event: Proto.ConfigFileDiagnosticEvent): void {
   253→		// See https://github.com/microsoft/TypeScript/issues/10384
   254→		const body = event.body;

    16→function diagnosticsEquals(a: vscode.Diagnostic, b: vscode.Diagnostic): boolean {
    17→	if (a === b) {
    18→		return true;
    19→	}
    20→
    21→	return a.code === b.code
    22→		&& a.message === b.message
    23→		&& a.severity === b.severity
    24→		&& a.source === b.source
    25→		&& a.range.isEqual(b.range)
    26→		&& arrays.equals(a.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, b.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, (a, b) => {
    27→			return a.message === b.message
    28→				&& a.location.range.isEqual(b.location.range)
    29→				&& a.location.uri.fsPath === b.location.uri.fsPath;
    30→		})
    31→		&& arrays.equals(a.tags || arrays.empty, b.tags || arrays.empty);
    32→}

	private setupFileWatcher(): vscode.Disposable {

		// Watch TypeScript/JavaScript files in the workspace
		for (const folder of vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders || []) {

				new vscode.RelativePattern(folder, '**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx,mts,cts,mjs,cjs}'),
				true,  // ignoreCreateEvents

				false  // ignoreDeleteEvents

+	private setupFileWatcher(): vscode.Disposable {
+		const watchers: vscode.Disposable[] = [];
+
+		// Watch TypeScript/JavaScript files in the workspace
+		for (const folder of vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders || []) {
+			const fileWatcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(
+				new vscode.RelativePattern(folder, '**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx,mts,cts,mjs,cjs}'),
+				true,  // ignoreCreateEvents
+				false, // ignoreChangeEvents
+				false  // ignoreDeleteEvents
+			);
+
+			fileWatcher.onDidChange(uri => {
+				this.onFileChanged(uri);
+			});
+
+			fileWatcher.onDidDelete(uri => {
+				this.onFileDeleted(uri);
+			});
+
+			watchers.push(fileWatcher);
+		}
+
+		// Return a disposable that disposes all watchers
+		return {
+			dispose: () => {
+				watchers.forEach(w => w.dispose());
+			}
+		};
+	}

147-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully implemented the fix for stale TypeScript diagnostics after Git branch switches. Here's a comprehensive summary of the implementation:

## Implementation Summary

### Problem
Users were seeing stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer had errors still showed old errors until the user manually opened and edited each file.

### Root Cause
The diagnostics pipeline was only refreshing on in-editor text changes, not when files changed on the file system (from Git operations).

### Solution Implemented

I've added file system change detection to the TypeScript extension that automatically clears stale diagnostics and requests re-analysis when files change on disk.

#### Changes Made:

**1. `languageFeatures/diagnostics.ts` - DiagnosticsManager**
- Added `onFileChanged(file: vscode.Uri)` method
- Clears stale diagnostics for files that change on disk
- Leverages existing `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile()` method

**2. `typeScriptServiceClientHost.ts` - TypeScriptServiceClientHost**
- Added `setupFileWatcher()` method that creates file system watchers for TypeScript/JavaScript files
- Watches all file extensions: `.ts`, `.tsx`, `.js`, `.jsx`, `.mts`, `.cts`, `.mjs`, `.cjs`
- Added `onFileChanged()` handler:
  - Notifies the appropriate LanguageProvider
  - Requests TypeScript server re-analysis via `getErr()`
- Added `onFileDeleted()` handler:
  - Clears diagnostics when files are deleted

**3. `languageProvider.ts` - LanguageProvider**
- Added `onFileChanged()` method that delegates to DiagnosticsManager
- Added `onFileDeleted()` method that clears file diagnostics

### How It Works

1. **File System Watcher Setup**: When the TypeScript service starts, a file watcher is created for each workspace

2. EDIT /workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/typeScriptServiceClientHost.ts
Before
		this.client.onTsServerStarted(() => {
			this.triggerAllDiagnostics();
		});

		vscode.workspace.onDidChangeConfiguration(this.configurationChanged, this, this._disposables);
		this.configurationChanged();
		this._register(new LogLevelMonitor(context));
	}
After
		this.client.onTsServerStarted(() => {
			this.triggerAllDiagnostics();
		});

		vscode.workspace.onDidChangeConfiguration(this.configurationChanged, this, this._disposables);
		this.configurationChanged();
		this._register(new LogLevelMonitor(context));

		// Watch for file system changes (e.g., from git operations) and refresh diagnostics
		this._register(this.setupFileWatcher());
	}

	private setupFileWatcher(): vscode.Disposable {
		const watchers: vscode.Disposable[] = [];

		// Watch TypeScript/JavaScript files in the workspace
		for (const folder of vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders || []) {
			const fileWatcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(
				new vscode.RelativePattern(folder, '**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx,mts,cts,mjs,cjs}'),
				true,  // ignoreCreateEvents
				false, // ignoreChangeEvents
				false  // ignoreDeleteEvents
			);

			fileWatcher.onDidChange(uri => {
				this.onFileChanged(uri);
			});

			fileWatcher.onDidDelete(uri => {
				this.onFileDeleted(uri);
			});

			watchers.push(fileWatcher);
		}

		// Return a disposable that disposes all watchers
		return {
			dispose: () => {
				watchers.forEach(w => w.dispose());
			}
		};
	}

	private onFileChanged(uri: vscode.Uri): void {
		// When a file changes on disk, clear stale diagnostics and request re-analysis
		for (const language of this.languages) {
			if (language.handlesUri(uri)) {
				language.onFileChanged(uri);
				break;
			}
		}

		// Request the TypeScript server to re-analyze this file
		this.client.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri]);
	}

	private onFileDeleted(uri: vscode.Uri): void {
		// When a file is deleted, clear its diagnostics
		for (const language of this.languages) {
			if (language.handlesUri(uri)) {
				language.onFileDeleted(uri);
				break;
			}
		}
	}

After
	public configFileDiagnosticsReceived(file: vscode.Uri, diagnostics: vscode.Diagnostic[]): void {
		this.client.diagnosticsManager.configFileDiagnosticsReceived(file, diagnostics);
	}

	public onFileChanged(file: vscode.Uri): void {
		// When a file changes on disk, clear stale diagnostics
		this.client.diagnosticsManager.onFileChanged(file);
	}

	public onFileDeleted(file: vscode.Uri): void {
		// When a file is deleted, clear its diagnostics
		this.client.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(file);
	}

	private get _diagnosticLanguage() {
		return this.description.diagnosticLanguage;
	}
